### 7100 - 7109 Social Democratic Events ###

country_event = { # Successful Propaganda Campaign
	id = 7100
	title = "EVT_7100_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_7100_DESC"
	picture = "ideology_socdem_pic"
	allow_multiple_instances = yes
	trigger = {
		has_country_modifier = propaganda_pro_socdem		# Pro-socdem Propaganda
		ideology = social_democrat				# Sanity check - do not fire if not socdem
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 48				# MTTH of four years
		modifier = {				# Consciousness Debuffs
			factor = 1.2
			average_consciousness = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			average_consciousness = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			average_consciousness = 6
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			average_consciousness = 8
		}
		modifier = {				# Militancy Debuffs
			factor = 1.2
			average_militancy = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			average_militancy = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			average_militancy = 6
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			average_militancy = 8
		}
		modifier = {				# Technology Buffs - Communications and Media
			factor = 0.9
			broadcasting = 1		# Broadcasting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			digital_media = 1		# Digital Media
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			the_internet = 1		# The Internet
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			web_20 = 1			# Web 2.0.
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			augmented_reality = 1		# Augmented Reality
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			virtual_reality = 1		# Virtual Reality
		}
		modifier = {				# Technology Buffs - Sociology
			factor = 0.9
			postmodernism = 1		# Postmodernism
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			reconstructivism = 1		# Reconstructivism
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			digital_sociology = 1		# Digital Sociology
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			neostructuralism = 1		# Neostructuralism
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			hephaestism = 1			# Hephaestism
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			super_sociology = 1		# Super-Sociology
		}
		modifier = {				# Technology Buffs - Psychology
			factor = 0.9
			cognitive_psychology = 1	# Cognitive Psychology
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			evolutionary_psychology = 1	# Evolutionary Psychology
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			digital_psychology = 1		# Digital Psychology
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			neuropsychology = 1		# Neuropsychology
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			artificial_psychology = 1	# Artificial Psychology
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			superintelligence = 1		# Superintelligence
		}
		modifier = {				# Press Rights
			factor = 0.75
			press_rights = state_press	# State Press good
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			press_rights = free_press	# Free Press bad
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVT_7100_OPTA"
		remove_country_modifier = propaganda_pro_socdem		# Remove propaganda
		random_list = {						# Randomized general ideology boost
			5 = {
				any_pop = {
					ideology = {
						factor = 0.05
						value = social_democrat
					}
				}
			}
			20 = {
				any_pop = {
					ideology = {
						factor = 0.10
						value = social_democrat
					}
				}
			}
			50 = {
				any_pop = {
					ideology = {
						factor = 0.15
						value = social_democrat
					}
				}
			}
			20 = {
				any_pop = {
					ideology = {
						factor = 0.20
						value = social_democrat
					}
				}
			}
			5 = {
				any_pop = {
					ideology = {
						factor = 0.25
						value = social_democrat
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_social_strata_target	# Clear all minor event flags
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_govt_employees_target
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_education_target
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_armed_forces_target
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_con_mil_target
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_diplo_prestige_target
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_close_ideologies_target
	}
}
country_event = { # Target Social Strata
	id = 7101
	title = "EVT_7101_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_7101_DESC"
	picture = "propaganda_socdem_social_strata_pic"
	allow_multiple_instances = yes
	trigger = {
		has_country_modifier = propaganda_pro_socdem			# Pro-socdem Propaganda
		NOT = { has_country_flag = propaganda_social_strata_target }	# Hasn't happened yet
		ideology = social_democrat					# Sanity check - do not fire if not socdem
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 36				# MTTH of three years
		modifier = {				# Consciousness Debuffs
			factor = 1.2
			average_consciousness = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			average_consciousness = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			average_consciousness = 6
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			average_consciousness = 8
		}
		modifier = {				# Technology Buffs - Communications and Media
			factor = 0.9
			broadcasting = 1		# Broadcasting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			digital_media = 1		# Digital Media
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			the_internet = 1		# The Internet
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			web_20 = 1			# Web 2.0.
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			augmented_reality = 1		# Augmented Reality
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			virtual_reality = 1		# Virtual Reality
		}
		modifier = {				# Technology Buffs - Psychology
			factor = 0.9
			cognitive_psychology = 1	# Cognitive Psychology
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			evolutionary_psychology = 1	# Evolutionary Psychology
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			digital_psychology = 1		# Digital Psychology
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			neuropsychology = 1		# Neuropsychology
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			artificial_psychology = 1	# Artificial Psychology
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			superintelligence = 1		# Superintelligence
		}
		modifier = {				# Press Rights
			factor = 0.75
			press_rights = state_press	# State Press good
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			press_rights = free_press	# Free Press bad
		}
		modifier = {				# Already had a target - Govt Employees
			factor = 1.3
			has_country_flag = propaganda_govt_employees_target
		}
		modifier = {				# Already had a target - Education
			factor = 1.3
			has_country_flag = propaganda_education_target
		}
		modifier = {				# Already had a target - Armed Forces
			factor = 1.3
			has_country_flag = propaganda_armed_forces_target
		}
		modifier = {				# Already had a target - Consciousness or Militancy
			factor = 1.3
			has_country_flag = propaganda_con_mil_target
		}
		modifier = {				# Already had a target - Foreign Affairs
			factor = 1.3
			has_country_flag = propaganda_diplo_prestige_target
		}
		modifier = {				# Already had a target - Close ideologies
			factor = 1.3
			has_country_flag = propaganda_close_ideologies_target
		}
		modifier = {				# Anything but limited or no agency
			factor = 0.67
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = defense_intel_domestic
				has_country_modifier = defense_intel_foreign
				has_country_modifier = defense_intel_military
				has_country_modifier = defense_intel_political
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVT_7101_OPTA"					# Upper Class
		set_country_flag = propaganda_social_strata_target	# Set flag to stop from repeating
		rich_strata = {
			ideology = {
				factor = 0.05
				value = social_democrat
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }				# Elites are low priority
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVT_7101_OPTB"					# Middle Class
		set_country_flag = propaganda_social_strata_target	# Set flag to stop from repeating
		middle_strata = {
			ideology = {
				factor = 0.05
				value = social_democrat
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 3 }				# Middle class is avg priority
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVT_7101_OPTC"					# Lower Class
		set_country_flag = propaganda_social_strata_target	# Set flag to stop from repeating
		poor_strata = {
			ideology = {
				factor = 0.05
				value = social_democrat
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 5 }				# Lower classes are high priority
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVT_7101_OPTD"					# No preference
		set_country_flag = propaganda_social_strata_target	# Set flag to stop from repeating
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				rich_strata = {
					ideology = {
						factor = 0.05
						value = social_democrat
					}
				}
			}
			50 = { rich_strata = { consciousness = 0.5 } }
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				middle_strata = {
					ideology = {
						factor = 0.05
						value = social_democrat
					}
				}
			}
			50 = { middle_strata = { consciousness = 0.5 } }
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				poor_strata = {
					ideology = {
						factor = 0.05
						value = social_democrat
					}
				}
			}
			50 = { poor_strata = { consciousness = 0.5 } }
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }				# Sometimes just have some random fun with it
	}
}

country_event = { # Target Academia
	id = 7103
	title = "EVT_7103_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_7103_DESC"
	picture = "propaganda_socdem_education_pic"
	allow_multiple_instances = yes
	trigger = {
		has_country_modifier = propaganda_pro_socdem			# Pro-socdem Propaganda
		NOT = { has_country_flag = propaganda_education_target }	# Hasn't happened yet
		ideology = social_democrat					# Sanity check - do not fire if not socdem
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 36				# MTTH of three years

			evolutionary_psychology = 1	# Evolutionary Psychology

			has_country_modifier = defense_intel_political
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVT_7103_OPTA"					# Educators
		set_country_flag = propaganda_education_target		# Set flag to stop from repeating
		clergymen = {
			ideology = {
				factor = 0.10
				value = social_democrat
			}
		}
		clergymen = {						# Purge dissenters out
			limit = {
				OR = {
					militancy = 7
					consciousness = 7
				}
			}
			pop_type = artisans				# They don't get killed, just become self-employed
		}
		any_pop = {						# Broad-scope political education
			ideology = {
				factor = 0.03
				value = social_democrat
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {					# Increase odds if radical dictatorship
				factor = 5
				OR = {
					government = communist_state
					government = theo_dictatorship
					government = ultranat_dictatorship
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVT_7103_OPTB"					# Researchers
		set_country_flag = propaganda_education_target		# Set flag to stop from repeating
		clergymen = {
			ideology = {
				factor = 0.10
				value = social_democrat
			}
		}
		any_pop = {						# Broad-scope political education
			ideology = {
				factor = 0.03
				value = social_democrat
			}
		}
		years_of_research = -0.10				# Sideline other research topics
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {					# Increase odds if moderate dictatorship
				factor = 5
				OR = {
					government = socialist_dictatorship
					government = minarchist_state
					government = eco_state
					government = nat_dictatorship
					government = theo_dictatorship
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVT_7103_OPTC"					# Academic Curriculum
		set_country_flag = propaganda_education_target		# Set flag to stop from repeating
		clergymen = {
			ideology = {
				factor = 0.10
				value = social_democrat
			}
		}
		any_pop = {						# Broad-scope political education
			ideology = {
				factor = 0.03
				value = social_democrat
			}
		}
		any_pop = { literacy = -0.05 }				# Sideline other education topics
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {					# Increase odds if biased democracy
				factor = 5
				OR = {
					government = limited_democracy
					government = socialist_democracy
					government = auth_democracy
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVT_7103_OPTD"					# No preference
		set_country_flag = propaganda_education_target		# Set flag to stop from repeating
		clergymen = {
			ideology = {
				factor = 0.05
				value = social_democrat
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {					# Increase odds if free-ish democracy
				factor = 5
				OR = {
					government = defensive_democracy
					government = democracy
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

					}
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_social_strata_target	# Clear all minor event flags
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_govt_employees_target
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_education_target
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_armed_forces_target
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_con_mil_target
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_diplo_prestige_target
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_close_ideologies_target
	}
}

		}
	}
	option = {

			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_social_strata_target	# Clear all minor event flags
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_govt_employees_target
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_education_target
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_armed_forces_target
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_con_mil_target
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_diplo_prestige_target
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_close_ideologies_target
	}
}

		ai_chance = { factor = 3 }				# Middle class is avg priority
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVT_7191_OPTC"					# Lower Class

			ideology = {
				factor = 0.05

			}
		}

	}

				rich_strata = {
					ideology = {
						factor = 0.05
						value = ultranationalist
					}
				}
			}
			50 = { rich_strata = { consciousness = 0.5 } }

			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_social_strata_target	# Clear all minor event flags
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_govt_employees_target
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_education_target
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_armed_forces_target
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_con_mil_target
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_diplo_prestige_target
		clr_country_flag = propaganda_close_ideologies_target
	}
}
